posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:Located in Beijing, I took my ten-year-old daughter to Nanjing for a trip during the Qingming Festival. I chose VOCO, which has a good location and is relatively new. The overall experience is very good. The hotel building is not very big, but it has a five-star style. The price has increased during the holiday. It should be less than 1,300 or 1,400 yuan for a normal stay, which is very cost-effective. I stayed for three days and chose a room with breakfast. The buffet breakfast is relatively rich and has many categories. The taste is basically OK, but the bread and fried dough sticks are not very delicious. Because I have requirements for hair dryers (it must be Dyson, otherwise I have to bring my own Dyson), I specially chose the City View Exclusive King Bed, which is a Dyson hair dryer. If you have requirements for hair dryers, you should confirm with the hotel that not all room types are Dyson. The room is very clean. After all, it has not been opened for a long time. The facilities are very new. Hot water bathing is very comfortable, and it is also very quiet and soundproof. But we opened the window for a while, and there seemed to be mosquitoes, which bit my daughter a few bags. Because we only stayed for three days, we didn‚Äôt ask for electric mosquito coils. Summer is coming soon. Friends who stay here need to pay attention to the problem of mosquitoes when opening windows, because we live on the seventh floor, and the hotel has a total of ten floors, which is not very high, and mosquitoes may fly up easily.
üìçSpecial note on location: Really great!
10 minutes walk from the Presidential Palace
5 minutes walk from 1912 Block
Downstairs is the subway station Fuqiao Station. Although we didn't take the subway, it was really convenient. We only played for three days. If the time is long, I think we will definitely take the subway later.
There is KFC downstairs from the hotel
There is Cha Baidao 50 meters in front of the hotel
The street downstairs is very prosperous, with various small shops and convenience stores for convenient needs
